Mac NID 6

NID 6 is 'Quicksand-Light', Everything looks good.

Quicksand Light Regular (Quicksand-Light.ttf)

name

MS NID 16/17

MS NID 16 + NID 17 should match NID 1 (+2).
Otherwise cross platform compatibility does not work between Mac (uses NID 16+17) and Windows (uses NID 1+2). (Jan 2019)

NID 16 'Quicksand' + 'Space' + NID 17 'Light' = NID 1 'Quicksand Light'.

Pass

Quicksand Medium Regular (Quicksand-Medium.ttf)

name

MS NID 16/17

MS NID 16 + NID 17 should match NID 1 (+2).
Otherwise cross platform compatibility does not work between Mac (uses NID 16+17) and Windows (uses NID 1+2). (Jan 2019)

NID 16 'Quicksand' + 'Space' + NID 17 'Medium' = NID 1 'Quicksand Medium'.

Pass

Quicksand Bold (Quicksand-Bold.ttf)

name

Mac NID 6

Mac NID 6, PostScript Name check for illegal characters.
Monotype uses NID 6 for creating CSS classes for their demo HTML. The following characters cause issues in the CSS code: '
, , , &, _, [, ], (, ), {, }, <, >, /, \, %'

NID 6 is 'Quicksand-Bold', Everything looks good.

Pass

Quicksand Bold (Quicksand-Bold.ttf)

name

MS NID 6

MS NID 6, PostScript Name check for illegal characters.
Monotype uses NID 6 for creating CSS classes for their demo HTML. The following characters cause issues in the CSS code: '
, , , &, _, [, ], (, ), {, }, <, >, /, \, %'

NID 6 is 'Quicksand-Bold', Everything looks good.
